function loadmap(){
	var bounds = new google.maps.LatLngBounds();
	var isDraggable = $(document).width() > 480 ? true : false;
	var marker;
	var myOptions = {
		zoom: 18,
		center: new google.maps.LatLng(35.6459439, 139.7120191),
		scrollwheel: false,
		draggable: isDraggable,
		mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP
	}
	
	var map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById("map"),myOptions);
	var image = new google.maps.MarkerImage("https://d418bv7mr3wfv.cloudfront.net/s3/W1siZiIsImNvbXBpbGVkX3RoZW1lX2Fzc2V0cy9zcGVjaWFsaXplZC1ncm91cC9wbmcvbWFwLW1hcmtlci5wbmciXV0", null, null, null);
	var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
		draggable: false,
		scrollwheel: false,
		raiseOnDrag: false,
		icon: image,
		animation: google.maps.Animation.DROP,
		map: map,
		position: new google.maps.LatLng(35.6459439, 139.7120191)
	  });
}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
	loadmap();
});

<script>
  window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
  
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ 
  
    if ($(".volcanic-form").length > 0 || $('#logo-upload-form').length > 0) {
      $.getScript( "/javascripts/jquery.iframe-transport.js" );
      $.getScript( "/javascripts/jquery.remotipart.js" );
    } 
    
    $('.volcanic-form').each( function() {
  
      var form_id = $(this).data("form-id");
      var article_permalink = $(this).data("article-permalink");
  
      $(this).replaceWith("<div class='form_" + form_id + "'>Loading form...</div>");
      
  
      var url = "/liquid/forms/" + form_id + "?locale=ja";
  
      if (article_permalink !== undefined) { url += "&permalink=" + article_permalink; }
  
      $.ajax({
        url: url,
        success:function(data) {
          $(".form_" + form_id ).html(data);
        },
        dataType: "html"
      });
      
    });
  
    $('.secure-volcanic-download').each( function() {
      var download_id = $(this).data("download-id");
      var $element = $(this);
      $.ajax({
        url: "/liquid/uploads/" + download_id,
        success:function(data) {
          $element.find("a").attr("href",data.url);
          $element.find("a").attr("target","_blank");
        },
        dataType: "json"
      });
      
    });
  });
</script>

<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
      // SET COOKIE IF DOESNT EXIST
    if (document.cookie.indexOf("volcanic_saved_jobs_id") < 0) {
      document.cookie = "volcanic_saved_jobs_id=" + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2) + "-" + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2) + "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT; path=/";
    };
  
    //LOOP SAVED JOBS
    $.getJSON( "/api/v1/users/saved_jobs.json?locale=ja", function( data ) {
      var items = [];
  
      $.each( data['saved_jobs'], function( key, val ) {
        //IF SAVED JOBS DROPDOWN LIST EXISTS
        if ($("ul[data-saved-jobs-list]").length){
          var item = "<li data-job-id='" + val['job'].id + "'><a href='" + val['job'].job_url + "'>" + val['job'].job_title + "</a></li>";
          items.push(item);
        };
        
        if ($("a#save_job_" + val['job'].id).length){
          $("a#save_job_" + val['job'].id).html(data['unsave_text']);
          $("a#save_job_" + val['job'].id).attr("href", val['job'].job_url + "/unsave_job");
        }
      });
  
      //IF SAVED JOBS DROPDOWN LIST EXISTS  --> POPULATE LIST
      if ($("ul[data-saved-jobs-list]").length){
        if (items.length > 0){
          $("ul[data-saved-jobs-list]").html(items.join( "" ));
        };
        $("span[data-saved-jobs-count]").html(items.length);
      };
    }); 
  });
</script>
